Program support is provided on musescore.org.\r\n\r\n\r\nFeatures supported by MuseScore include:\r\n\r\n* Unlimited score length\r\n* Unlimited number of staves per system\r\n* Up to four independent voices per staff\r\n* Score creation wizard and templates\r\n* Guitar, bass, ukulele, lute tablature\r\n* Automatic part extraction and transposition\r\n* Repeats, including segnos, codas, and measure repeats\r\n* Dynamics, articulations, and other expression markings, with playback support for most\r\n* Custom text markings\r\n* Lyrics\r\n* Chord symbols\r\n* Jazz notation, including lead sheets, slash notation and a “handwritten” font for text\r\n* Swing and shuffle playback\r\n* Mixer for instrument levels and effects\r\n* Percussion notation\r\n* Early music notation\r\n* Cross-staff beaming\r\n* Import of graphics\r\n* Custom key signatures\r\n* Additive time signatures\r\n* User-defined score styles\r\n\r\nMost elements in MuseScore are laid out automatically but can also be positioned manually. The capabilities of MuseScore can be extended via plugins, and the growing repository on musescore.org contains many plugins submitted by users.\r\n\r\nMuseScore includes a set of sounds that reproduce common instruments (as defined by General MIDI) without taking up a lot of disk space or memory, but you can also substitute any SoundFont you prefer for a wider variety of sounds or for more realism.\r\n\r\nMuseScore can import and export MIDI and MusicXML files, and it can also import from Capella and several other programs. MuseScore can export to PDF, PNG, and other graphic formats, to WAV and other audio formats, or to Lilypond for an alternative layout and print With a 360° view of your business information at your finger-tips, you can stay on top of things when dealing with your customers. \r\n\r\nElegantly Simple\r\nWe use the elegantly simple \"Cards-and-Paper\" metaphor to design our user interface. The \"Cards\" is on the left-hand side of the app to reference a list of customers, inventory items and pricing. You can reference the \"Cards\" to add inventory items onto the \"Paper\" (which is the invoice) on the right. This is a metaphor that most of us, who need to issue invoices, can understand, visualize and associate with. We gleaned this metaphor from previous experiences where we successfully helped fast-growing companies transform their on the go manual \"Cards-and-Paper\" invoice issuance to that of a fully automated one using our software. With this elegantly simple user interface, we hope to enable you create any invoice within 10 seconds. \r\n\r\nProfessional invoice templates to choose from or customize!\r\nYou can choose an invoice template that comes with Invoice 360 without the need to create one from scratch.
